### Post by mrdiego on 2009-01-23
**Hello**

I was bored with Gnome so I checked out Kubuntu (KDE 4.2 RC1). I love it - it's pretty modern and full with new innovations. Firefox and Evolution for example I installed them without the GTK-recommends and added in the .gtk-kd4-File that I am using "Human-O2". So I can enjoy my human-feeling in KDE with every kind of application ;)
I know Gnome is more stable and XCFE is the fastest... but very very old style and not so flexible like KDE for example.
But this is like always a opinion ... my opinion is that. ;)

So I have KDE, I will adjust my Icon-Set for it ... ;D

Bye,
mrdiego

### Post by Shippou on 2009-01-24
Hello guys...

Theme: All Black*
Wallpaper: Gabumon**
Icons: see theme explanation below
Programs: Conky***, two gnome-panels****

As a bonus, attached also is my new Firefox theme.*****

*All Black is the name of the theme I made with the following: (made via Appearance Preferences):
Controls: Aurora-Midnight
Colors: 
Windows: Background:#2C2C2C, Text:#FFFFFF
Input Boxes: Background:#121212, Text:#FFFFFF
Selected Items: Background:#5FBBFF, Text:#0C0C0C
Window Border: Moomex-Ultimatum
Icons: Oxygen
Pointer: DMZ(Black), Smallest size

**Gabumon screenshot from Digimon Adventure 01 ep 08

***Conky version 1.6.1
Conky Code:
```

# Generated by Conky GUI
# Check http://conkygui.sourceforge.net/
# For the latest version of Conky GUI

#11-Jan-09 12:02:03 PM
#
#

# Conky
background no
no_buffers no
out_to_console no
top_cpu_separate no
max_port_monitor_connections 256
cpu_avg_samples 3
net_avg_samples 3
total_run_times 0
update_interval 1
music_player_interval 3

# Text
uppercase no
override_utf8_locale yes
short_units no
pad_percents -5
text_buffer_size 95
max_user_text 200001
font Nimbus Sans L:style=Regular Condensed
use_xft no
xftalpha 0.0
xftfont -*-tlwgtypewriter-*-r-normal-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

# Window
own_window yes
own_window_class Config
own_window_colour 660099
own_window_transparent yes
own_window_title Config
own_window_hints undecorated,below,above,sticky,skip_taskbar,skip_pager
own_window_type normal

# Graphics
double_buffer yes
draw_borders no
draw_graph_borders no
draw_shades yes
draw_outline no
stippled_borders 8
max_specials 511

# Layout
alignment top_right
gap_x 0
gap_y 0
maximum_width 1001
minimum_size 200 15
use_spacer left
border_margin 4
border_width 1

# Colors
default_color 000000
default_outline_color ffffff
default_shade_color c0c0c0
color0 ff0000
color1 0000ff
color2 ffff00
color3 00ff00
color4 ffafaf
color5 ffc800
color6 ff00ff
color7 00ffff
color8 808080
color9 404040

# Net

# stuff after 'TEXT' will be formatted on screen

TEXT
${color indigo}COMPUTER SPECS: 
CPU:
CPU FREQUENCY: ${freq_dyn_g} GHz
CPU USAGE: ${cpubar 10,70}

OS:
SYSTEM NAME: ${sysname}
KERNEL: ${kernel}

NETWORK SETTINGS: 
HOST NAME: ${nodename}
${color 7F00FF}
Eth0:
IP Address: ${addr eth0}
DL SPEED: ${downspeedgraph eth0 10,70} (${downspeed eth0}kB/s)  
UL SPEED: ${upspeedgraph eth0 10,70}(${upspeed eth0}kB/s) 
TOTAL DL: ${totaldown eth0}
TOTAL UL: ${totalup eth0}
${color blue}
Eth1:
IP Address: ${addr eth1}
DL SPEED: ${downspeedgraph eth1 10,70} (${downspeed eth1}kB/s)  
UL SPEED: ${upspeedgraph eth1 10,70}(${upspeed eth1}kB/s) 
TOTAL DL: ${totaldown eth1}
TOTAL UL: ${totalup eth1}
${color red}
Eth2:
IP Address: ${addr eth2}
DL SPEED: ${downspeedgraph eth2 10,70} (${downspeed eth2}kB/s)  
UL SPEED: ${upspeedgraph eth2 10,70}(${upspeed eth2}kB/s) 
TOTAL DL: ${totaldown eth2}
TOTAL UL: ${totalup eth2}
${color orange}
Eth3:
IP Address: ${addr eth3}
DL SPEED: ${downspeedgraph eth3 10,70} (${downspeed eth3}kB/s)  
UL SPEED: ${upspeedgraph eth3 10,70}(${upspeed eth3}kB/s) 
TOTAL DL: ${totaldown eth3}
TOTAL UL: ${totalup eth3}
${color brown}
Eth4:
IP Address: ${addr eth4}
DL SPEED: ${downspeedgraph eth4 10,70} (${downspeed eth0}kB/s)  
UL SPEED: ${upspeedgraph eth4 10,70}(${upspeed eth4}kB/s) 
TOTAL DL: ${totaldown eth4}
TOTAL UL: ${totalup eth4}
${color indigo}
DEMOGRAPHICS: 
TODAY: ${time}
SYSTEM UPTIME: ${uptime}

CONKY:
Version: ${conky_version} 
BD: ${conky_build_date}

```

****Gnome panel configs:
Lowest: Show Desktop Button, Windows Selector, Windows List, Clock, Workspace Switcher, Pointer Capture Applet
Leftmost (the smaller one, autohide activated): Wanda, Drawer, Tomboy, Main Menu, Nautilus Shortcut, Firefox, Force-Kill, Tracker, Volume Applet, Gnome-Do, Network Manager Applet, Pulse-Audio applet, Universal Access Applet

*****Firefox:
1. Install Stylish add-on.
2. Then, go to [www.userscripts.org](www.userscripts.org) and search for the following scripts:

a. Matrix - Global Style      <- makes all webpages have a black background and green text
b. about:blank - Dark Firefox  <- for displaying the blue Firefox logo at every blank tab
c. BlackMail (real black gmail Theme)
d. Firefox 3 - Chrome Theme  (Dark Gray) Tabs on Top   <- for Google Chrome styled tabs
e. Firefox 3 - Tab Tweaks
f. OneManga - Optimal Viewing
g. Yahoo! Wide BlackForest

### Post by el mariachi on 2009-01-24
> **andrek said:**
> Could you share your conky setup?
```
own_window yes
own_window_type desktop
own_window_transparent yes
own_window_colour 000000
own_window_hints undecorated,below,sticky,skip_taskbar,skip_pager
double_buffer yes
use_spacer none 
use_xft yes
uppercase yes
override_utf8_locale yes
xftfont ITC Avant Garde Gothic Std:size=40
#xftfont Neutra Text TF:book:size=40
update_interval 1.0
draw_shades no
draw_outline no
draw_borders no
stippled_borders 0
border_margin 0
border_width 0
default_color ffffff
own_window_transparent yes
minimum_size 1 1
maximum_width 200 
#alignment top_left
#alignment top_right
alignment bottom_left
#alignment bottom_right
gap_x 0
gap_y 10 

TEXT
${font ITC Avant Garde Gothic Std:bold:size=40}${time %d}${font}${time %b}
```

```
own_window yes
own_window_type desktop
own_window_transparent yes
own_window_colour 000000
own_window_hints undecorated,below,sticky,skip_taskbar,skip_pager
double_buffer yes
use_spacer none 
use_xft yes
override_utf8_locale yes
xftfont glisp 
update_interval 1.0
draw_shades no
draw_outline no
draw_borders no
stippled_borders 0
border_margin 0
border_width 0
default_color ffffff 
own_window_transparent yes
minimum_size 1 1
maximum_width 1440
alignment top_left
#alignment top_right
alignment bottom_left
#alignment bottom_right
gap_x 176
gap_y 38

TEXT
${color CBC760}CPU:${color} ${cpu}% ${color CBC760}Mem:${color} $memperc% ${color CBC760}Down:${color} ${downspeed eth0}Kb/s ${color CBC760}Up:${color} ${upspeed eth0}Kb/s
```

### Post by Giant Speck on 2009-01-26
> **pt123 said:**
> Thanks do you know the background behind this?

The version of the Murrine engine you are using is probably the SVN version, which is the bleeding-edge, ever-changing version of the Murrine version.

Cimi, the author of the Murrine engine updates the engine every now and then.  Since the first SVN version, the "style" option has been changed to "profile."

Thanks. That's just a superkaramba widget that I made. It's really simple. I just made some pictures of the numbers 0-9 and added shadows and reflection. All the widget does is gets the time from the date command and displays the appropriate images in the right places. Here's a link:

### Post by eightmillion on 2009-01-26
> **Daisuke_Aramaki said:**
> always wanted to ferment my own beer! :D

I don't know about fermenting beer, but you can sing along.

```
bo="bottle";be="of beer";ta="Take one down and pass it around";wa="on the wall";i=99;\
while [ "$i" != 0 ]; do printf "$i $bo`[ $i != 1 ] && echo s` $be $wa,\n$i $bo`[ $i != 1 ] &&\
 echo s` $be.\n$ta, `[ $((i-1)) != 0 ] && echo $((i-1)) || echo "no more"` $bo`[ $i != 2 ] &&\
 echo s` $be.\n\n"  ;i=$((i-1));done;  printf "No more ${bo}s $be $wa,\nno more ${bo}s $be.\nGo to the store and buy some more, 99 ${bo}s $be $wa.\n"
```

---

### Post by Daisuke_Aramaki on 2009-01-26

```
bo="bottle";be="of beer";ta="Take one down and pass it around";wa="on the wall";i=99;\
while [ "$i" != 0 ]; do printf "$i $bo`[ $i != 1 ] && echo s` $be $wa,\n$i $bo`[ $i != 1 ] &&\
 echo s` $be.\n$ta, `[ $((i-1)) != 0 ] && echo $((i-1)) || echo "no more"` $bo`[ $i != 2 ] &&\
 echo s` $be.\n\n"  ;i=$((i-1));done;  printf "No more ${bo}s $be $wa,\nno more ${bo}s $be.\nGo to the store and buy some more, 99 ${bo}s $be $wa.\n"
```

### Post by eightmillion on 2009-01-27
> **BazookaAce said:**
> What theme is that? It's f****** awsome ;) Hope you can give me some details about it!

Thanks. Here's the info:

KDE 4.2.60 (KDE 4.3 >= 20090116)
Wallpaper: [http://shunnabunich.deviantart.com/art/Happy-Little-Feelers-109099707](http://shunnabunich.deviantart.com/art/Happy-Little-Feelers-109099707)
Font: Segoe
Widget style: Bespin
Window decoration: [http://kde-look.org/content/show.php/Dworkin+Dark?content=95350](http://kde-look.org/content/show.php/Dworkin+Dark?content=95350)
Clock: [http://kde-look.org/content/show.php/3D+Desktop+Clock?content=95681](http://kde-look.org/content/show.php/3D+Desktop+Clock?content=95681)

The dock is cairo dock and the icons are custom. The music widget is custom too, but I have a similar one on kde-look [here.]("http://kde-look.org/content/show.php/Amarok+2+Simple?content=93541") Also, my window decoration in the screenshot is slightly darker than the one on kde-look. You can make it the same by going into the deco directory and running "**mogrify -modulate 80% ***".  On kde-look, I have a version of the same decoration for emerald too.

### Post by raul_ on 2009-01-28
> **armageddon08 said:**
> Just installed KDE 4.2 - awesome:)

But I still haven't figured out how Raul got the menu bar at the top of the screen.

Did you install Bespin? If so, unlock widgets and add xbar to a panel. To get the menu bar at the top effect, add a slim panel to the top and add the xbar plasmoid to it ;)

---

### Post by chucky chuckaluck on 2009-01-28
> **dannytatom said:**
> Looks sexy, have a few (probably obvious) questions though.

1) I'm looking into XMonad and how do you open apps with it (is there a menu like openbox's?

you need to install dmenu. i think alt+p starts it (top of the screen). you begin typing the app you want and the app will be highlighted in the menubar after a few letters. hit 'enter', the menubar disappears and the app opens.

---

### Post by Daisuke_Aramaki on 2009-01-28
> **dannytatom said:**
> Looks sexy, have a few (probably obvious) questions though.

1) I'm looking into XMonad and how do you open apps with it (is there a menu like openbox's?)

2) What music player is that?

3) How did you get your terminal so colorful?

1.chucky is right. dmenu can be activated by Alt+P and the program to run can be typed in. You can also assign a special key in the xmonad.hs file, which is the main config file for any other Run program, like gmrun for instance. 

2. That must be ncmpcpp

3. Colors, fonts, transparencies presence or absence of scrollbars etc., can be set in the .Xdefaults file and terminals like xterm, urxvt, aterm etc., can read from that. But if you intend to use gnome terminal or xfce4 terminal etc., you can always set different options in your .bashrc or .zshrc depending on the shell you mostly use. Besides if you use vim (as it is seen in the screen), you can also use different color schemes for that!

Hope that helps and hope Thanapalan doesn't mind!

---
